Recent Rice Shortage in Hunan Province 82

Rice prices have also risen to 19 yuan per stone; A Changsha dispatch reports that Hunan Province is a rice-producing region with a large amount of rice exports annually. The budgeted rice donation income is 2 million yuan, but in reality, it always exceeds that amount by more than double. The average rice price per stone (148 catties) is below 12 yuan, which is cheaper than any port along the Yangtze River. However, recently, it has developed into an extremely serious shortage, with prices reaching 19 yuan per stone, and even with money, there is no rice to buy. There are two main reasons for this rice shortage: first, the government excessively issued rice permits last year, only seeking income from the permit fees, resulting in the transportation of grain from the interior and making it difficult to regulate the soaring rice prices; second, unscrupulous merchants took the opportunity to hoard and speculate, hindering purchases and seeking profits. Government officials failed to maintain order properly, giving unscrupulous merchants the opportunity to control the market and causing today's shortage. More than a month ago, the rice price in Changsha City rose to over 10 yuan per stone, causing panic among the poor, who lamented the high price of rice. Government officials, gentry, and business circles, also recognizing the impact on people's livelihoods, immediately initiated the organization of a People's Food Maintenance Association, electing eleven members to be responsible for regulating the people's food supply. At that time, an investigation revealed that there were a total of over 300,000 stones of stored grain in the provincial capital, which was only enough to meet the needs until the new harvest. Therefore, a clear order was issued: (1) to prohibit the shipping of grain by river, train, or transport of grain out of the provincial capital; (2) starting from June 1st, to prohibit milling of cooked rice and only allow pushing and producing Qi rice (i.e., only removing the husk), with the intention of avoiding waste of grain and increasing the production of Qi rice to reduce rice prices; (3) to investigate poor households and prepare for subsidized sales; (4) to purchase Saigon rice to provide relief. Unexpectedly, the clear order had the opposite effect. Within one or two days, Qi rice suddenly rose to 12-13 yuan. Poor people carrying baskets on their shoulders often walked all day without being able to buy rice, while cooked rice rose to 18-19 yuan. The wealthy, accustomed to luxury, were unwilling to eat coarse food. Upon hearing the news of the prohibition on milling cooked rice, they disregarded the high prices and purchased and stored several months' worth of grain in advance. Suddenly, the market demand exceeded the supply. Although each rice factory and stackyard was producing rice day and night and raising market prices, it was still insufficient to meet the purchases of the wealthy. As a result, the price of cooked rice was high, and there was no time to produce Qi rice. Even the small amount of Qi rice that was produced and sold on the market was mixed with sand, stones, chaff, and bran, making it inedible, and the price was also raised along with the price of cooked rice. In addition, rice merchants took the opportunity to secretly produce cooked rice and store it in high-rise buildings, selling it at high prices, and only displaying a small amount of Qi rice to meet market demand, resulting in even higher black market prices for rice (Qi rice at 15 yuan per stone, cooked rice at 20 yuan). In the meantime, due to Zhang Gui's invasion of Hunan, military affairs were urgent, and there was no time to take care of the people's food crisis. Until recently, the poor had nothing to eat, and an investigation revealed that there were still over 200,000 stones of grain stored in the provincial capital, clearly indicating that unscrupulous merchants were hoarding and speculating, controlling the market for profit. Therefore, there were numerous petitions to the government to maintain the people's food supply, investigate unscrupulous merchants, and investigate the persons in charge of the People's Food Maintenance Association. As a result, Wei Suzhong, the commander of the Changsha Garrison, sent a letter to the Maintenance Association, saying, "Our army has restored order in Changsha and quelled the situation. We have long been preparing to maintain the people's food supply, but day by day, it continues to increase. The reason for this is that unscrupulous merchants are manipulating the market, hoarding goods, and even openly selling Qi rice while secretly selling cooked rice at higher prices. The situation is ambiguous. Although it is said to be maintenance, it is actually an opportunity for merchants to profit. If strict rectification is not carried out, the poor will not be able to live, and a terrible situation will inevitably be created, endangering public security. It is appropriate to send a letter to your association, requesting that you quickly find a way to stabilize prices to maintain the people's food supply. If any unscrupulous merchants still dare to profit from it and deliberately control the market, once our department discovers it, they will be punished as disturbers of public order and will not be tolerated." At the same time, the provincial government also sent personnel to secretly investigate the rice market, strictly prohibiting price increases, and allocated 12,000 stones of stored grain from the provincial warehouse to the People's Food Maintenance Association to expedite subsidized sales. They also telegraphed Shanghai merchants to rush the shipment of Saigon rice to Hunan to provide relief. The Maintenance Association then convened an emergency meeting at 4:00 p.m. on the 26th, attended by ten people, including Xiao Laisheng, and elected Pi Zongrang as chairman. It was resolved that subsidized sales would be launched in advance on July 1st. Zhang Dacong and Luo Qingyun were appointed as directors of the Eastern District, Hu Junfu and Xie Jusheng were appointed as directors of the Southern District, Zhang Shurong and Cheng Qianhe were appointed as directors of the Western District, and Chen Liaosheng and Huang Peishi were appointed as directors of the Northern District, dividing the city into four districts for subsidized sales. Li Xi Zhuan and Yang Hengzhai were appointed as standing committee members for subsidized sales, Li Jingtao and Liu Boheng were appointed as finance committee members, Huang Zhizhou was appointed as a member of the purchasing committee for beans and grains, Wang Boqing, Xie Zixian, and Zhang Xiangquan were appointed as food distribution committee members and were responsible for milling grain, and Feng Gengtao, Ding Ziqin, and Xiong Fanzhou were appointed as investigation committee members. It was also stipulated that the subsidized sales would be carried out with a combination of rice and beans, with each adult receiving five he of rice and three he of beans per day, and each child receiving three he of rice and one he of beans per day, according to the registered list of poor households. Rice purchase certificates would be distributed directly to each district for daily purchases. It was estimated that there were over 93,000 poor households in the entire city. As for the Saigon rice to be purchased, it was limited to arriving in Hunan on July 1st and would be distributed at the purchase market price and shipping costs. Government agencies, organizations, or wealthy households would also be charged within 18 yuan. With these regulations, it may be possible to prevent an unexpected situation from developing (27th).

Jiangsu Entomological Bureau Tests Poison Bait for Locust Control 83

The use of poison bait to kill locusts is a common method in all locust-producing countries in the world. Since its establishment, the Jiangsu Entomological Bureau has conducted many tests, but the results have not been significant, so it has not been widely adopted. This is because the conditions in each locust-producing region are different, and the types of locusts are also different. What is suitable for one place may not be suitable for another. Since Chen Jiaxiang, the director of the Locust Research Institute of the Bureau, obtained considerable results in a test in Liuhe last year, he planned to conduct a large-scale test this year, designating Chongming as the test area. However, since the area of Chongming County was too large, it was changed to Bagua Island as the test area. Unexpectedly, this year there was a lot of rain, and the locust eggs on Bagua Island rotted and did not hatch. It was then heard that locusts were occurring in Chongming, so the Bureau immediately ordered Director Chen to lead researcher Huang Zhongqiang to Chongming with a large amount of white arsenic. However, the few locust nymphs in Chongming had already been eaten by ducks. Therefore, they conducted a test in Wangyang Village, Haimen on June 22. However, the ground was mostly water in the areas where there were locust nymphs, so poison bait could not be applied. They had no choice but to choose more than ten mu of land without water for the test. After 4:00 p.m. on the 23rd, three pounds of poison bait were applied per mu. The ratio of the mixture was one part white arsenic, one part brown sugar, thirty parts wheat bran, and twenty-five parts water (by weight). On the 24th, there were a few dead locust nymphs on the ground. On the 25th, there were more. On the morning of the 26th, an inspection revealed even more. The most numerous area had fifteen locust nymphs per square foot, with an average of about four locust nymphs per square foot. It was estimated that there were 24,000 dead locust nymphs per mu. Even the winged locusts that had emerged a few days ago had died. The effectiveness of the poison bait had not yet expired, but after a heavy thunderstorm in the middle of the night on the 25th, the poison bait was completely washed away, which was very regrettable. In addition, locust nymphs like to migrate, and many locust nymphs from watery areas migrated to the areas where poison bait had been applied. Also, locust nymphs need one or two days to die after eating poison bait. Before the toxicity takes effect, they often migrate to other places, making it difficult to calculate the percentage of locusts killed. Therefore, testing in that area was very unsuitable. It is now heard that Mr. Chen and others are about to leave Wangyang Village and go to other places to look for suitable locust-infested locations for testing, according to a local dispatch.

Police squad goes to Xin to drive out refugees. Yesterday, over three hundred refugees arrived in Xinzhuang Town. Men, women, old, and young were there. For a time, the people were nervous. The case has been reported to the county for investigation. The county government immediately appointed Secretary Zhang to go to the countryside for inspection yesterday. Punan Zhalin hailstorm causes disaster. On a certain day last month, the weather changed suddenly and a hailstorm fell. Farmers in Punan and other townships who planted cotton suffered a great blow. Farmers in Fengxian and Minhang were all sad. Although this county is a rice-producing area, Zhalin, which is part of the county, is located on the coast and has always been engaged in cotton planting. Since the hailstorm, the cotton plants have withered. This year's harvest is completely hopeless. The old farmers all said that fortunately, the hailstorm came early. If they could find cotton seeds to replant, they could still sprout. However, even if they are successful, the harvest will be greatly affected. However, it is heard that cotton seeds are in short supply and difficult to purchase. Therefore, the disaster in the third ward, which was the most severely affected, has been reported to the county government for investigation.

Jinshan 85

Bandit traces are found in all townships. Since last year, bandits have been rampant in this county, and robberies have been frequent. Local residents cannot bear it. Previously, Chen Zekuan, the director of the first district of the Provincial Water Police Corps, sent a team to Zhu to join the county police team to search for bandits in Qianjiawei and Kongjiaque. Several bandits were immediately arrested. Unexpectedly, there were more than ten bandits hiding in the home of Ling A-gui, the head of the Bochi Nunnery. When they saw the police team arriving, they first fired shots. A police officer from the county police team was shot and killed, and the bandits took the opportunity to escape. Afterwards, a lot of stolen goods were found in Ling A-gui's house, which was confirmed to be a bandit den, and it was burned down. Since then, the bandits' traces have been slightly restrained. However, before long, they saw that the police team had left and knew that there was nothing to fear, so they relapsed. As for Dianxiaqiao, Liujiawan, Bazhiqiao, Qianjiawei, Kongjiaque, Wanchunqiao, Xiaoshantang, Mingzhuan and other townships, bandit traces have been found in all of them recently. Their lairs are located near the townships, such as Nanjiao, Louqian, Caoan, Baimike, Sanqinggang, Lijiagangxia, etc. In addition to occupying temples and tombs, they have recently been forcibly occupying people's houses, moving and fleeing day and night. When the military police arrive, they have already heard the news and hid. Therefore, if you want to find the root cause, you must conduct strict investigation. It is also heard that a gang of bandits, Jin Fei, has more than one hundred members. They were originally active in other places, but now they have also joined the Taibao A-shu gang, so their power is becoming more and more rampant. The gang of bandits even paraded with full arms and fluttering red flags the day before. Then they went to Langxia Town and intimidated the merchants to extort 1,200 yuan. In addition, dozens of threatening letters have been received in various places, all of which were sent by Taibao A-shu and Xu A-jin through their subordinates Gu A-long, Xi Daoming, Dai Kechang, Zhang A-mu, and Wang A-jiu to extort thousands of yuan or hundreds of yuan, depending on the case.

Suzhou 86

Heavy Thunderstorm in Suzhou City

On the evening of the previous day (29th) around 6:00 or 7:00 p.m., there was a heavy thunderstorm in Suzhou City. The electric lights outside Lumu Gate went out at 7:18 p.m. and the streets were plunged into darkness for 27 minutes. They finally came back on at 7:45 p.m. Afterwards, it was discovered that the telephone lines were down in Jiejia Bridge, the eastern and western parts of the central market, and the areas outside the city, affecting as many as 150 or 160 households. Also, at 6:30 p.m., two particularly large claps of thunder struck. One of the wooden flagpoles in front of the old provincial government (i.e., the current Customs Superintendent's Office) on the left side was destroyed. The area about seven or eight feet below the dougong (bracket set) of the flagpole was struck, and the dougong fell to the ground in pieces. The broken wood that fell to the ground was about twenty or thirty feet long. At the same time, at the house of Hou Zhuang-sheng at No. 39 Songxianzhou Alley, a ball of fire the size of a washbasin appeared, emitting red light with purple and green hues. It came straight down through a crack in the bricks in the middle of the first rafter on the south side of the first bay of the house. It was only a few feet away from the bed and where people were standing. Afterwards, this ball of fire charged up towards the tip of the mountain wall next to the second bay of the house. Because the bricks were strong and thick, it could not break through immediately. It then moved horizontally along the roof, passing over the bottom of the bricks on the second bay of the house and striking the second beam of the third bay, breaking the house and flying away. Also, the house of Zhang Min-nong at No. 14 Niuyachang, behind Tongren Street, under Lumu Gate, collapsed, crushing the bed. Fortunately, the family was having dinner in the outer room and was not injured. In addition, there were many other incidents of collapsing houses and destruction.

Citywide Reorganization into Three Branch Bureaus

After the merger of the city's Public Security Bureau, the entire city was reorganized into three branch bureaus. The northeastern and northern districts were merged into the First Branch Bureau, with the bureau's address located in the northern district at the original location. The southwestern and southern districts were merged into the Second Branch Bureau, with the bureau's address located in the southern district at the original location. The district was renamed the Third Branch Bureau, with the bureau's address still located at the original location. The chiefs of each branch bureau and the inspectors of each branch police station were all announced yesterday (30th).

Solving a Robbery and Murder Case

On the evening of the 22nd of this month, Jiangbei bandits robbed the home of Dai Yongxing, a carpenter in Wangjiabang Village, Lingjinglang Township, Taipingqiao Township, which is part of the county. The robbers stole 120-130 yuan in foreign currency, three shi of wheat, and two shi of rice. At the time, Dai's wife resisted the robbers with an axe, but was instead slashed in the head. Dai Yongxing was slashed to death by the robbers on the spot. The local bailiff reported the case to the court and went to the village for an examination. Neighbors reported that Chen Xi from Yancheng was related to the case. At that time, Chen had fled. Chen's wife, Guo, was taken to the court for investigation and is on file. Yesterday (30th), Xu Fengshan, the detective of the Third District of the Water Police, led detectives Shao Yuanlong, Yang Baokang, Kong Qingchang, and Qian Jin to investigate. They learned that Chen Xi was hiding in the area outside Qimu Gate. At about 11:00 a.m., they secretly inquired at the Qiyilou Teahouse outside Qimu Gate. Chen Xi also arrived at the teahouse at 2:00 p.m. and was captured by Detective Xu and others. He was escorted back to the district headquarters, where District Chief Gong interrogated him on the spot. According to Chen Xi's confession, he is 50 years old, also known as Lao Chen. He has been buying and dismantling old houses in Taipingqiao Lingjinglang for his livelihood, and lives on a small boat. He has a total of three wives. The robbery of Dai Yongxing's house was committed by the Pan Changshan and Pan Guanghong brothers. They are also from Yancheng. He heard that they stole three shi of wheat, two shi of rice, and about 120-130 yuan in foreign currency. At that time, I was in Suzhou. After they robbed the loot, they went to Pan Guanghong's boat. Now they have escaped to the area of ​​Luxiang Hengjing. Now my wife has been arrested by the local court. This is really a injustice. Please have mercy, sir. After hearing the confession, District Chief Gong ordered that Chen Fei's wife had already been detained in the local court, so he immediately ordered that he be sent to the local court to handle the case together.

Changshu 89

Cai Yizhi's Incest Case

Bribery Leads to Detention. Cai Yizhi of Baoben Street in the city was sentenced to death by the county government for the matricide case in the winter of the year before last. Cai then filed an appeal. The Suzhou Higher Court, in order to clarify the truth, divided and summoned seven people, including Yue Guniang, Zhang Xiqing, and Lu Jusheng and Xu Zhensheng, police officers of the county government, to be tried on July 2. Jiang Kuiyuan, a Shanghai silk merchant (i.e., Wang Ziping), came to Chang from Shanghai on the 26th to Beishixin Street and contacted Xu Zhensheng, a police officer. He claimed that he was entrusted by Zhang Zhixuan, a lawyer from Ximenwai, Shanghai, to Chang specially to find a way to overthrow Cai Yizhi's previous confession. He asked Xu to greet the summoned police officers to testify in court and prove that Cai's previous confession was indeed a confession. If the previous confession was overturned, I would pay you 1,000 yuan on behalf of Cai. At that time, Xu falsely agreed. Wang then took out 60 yuan in banknotes and gave it to Xu as travel expenses to Suzhou. Xu then returned to the county to report. Stone trial judge issued a warrant and sent police to the Dafang Hotel where Jiang Kuiyuan was staying to arrest Jiang. After questioning, he confessed that he was introduced by a relative surnamed Shen who had a slight relationship with Cai Yizhi to the lawyer Zhang Zhirang and asked me to handle this matter and presented a letter from lawyer Zhang to Jiang and a list of the police officers who were contacted. During the court hearing, police officer Xu Zhensheng testified about Jiang Kuiyuan's bribery. Stone trial judge ordered Jiang to be detained. The next day (28th), he was brought back to court for questioning. He claimed that Cai Yizhi's third concubine, Cai Lishi (i.e., Yue Guniang), was my aunt. I have no relationship with the surnamed Shen. I came to Chang to clear the way for the police. Stone trial judge questioned and asked what was the method you thought of? Jiang replied that Lawyer Zhang came up with the idea and asked me to do the police bribery. The 60 yuan was given to me by Cai Lishi. After questioning, he was still detained.

Jiangyin 92

Investigation into the Case of the Company Commander Being Robbed of Military Pay: Wang Longdao, the company commander of the 8th Company, 2nd Battalion, 1st Regiment of the Chengcheng (Jiangyin) Garrison, was robbed of over 1,250 silver dollars of his April military pay on the evening of the 26th. Upon receiving the report, the regimental headquarters immediately dispatched Adjutant Zhu Youyun to Chengcheng to conduct an on-the-ground investigation. At the time, Guo Hongjin, a committee member assigned by the Ministry of Military Affairs, and Pan Yuan, the Director of the Military Supplies Department of the Capital Garrison Headquarters, were distributing pay for the garrison regiment along the Changzhou-Shanghai railway line. According to Mr. Jin from the regimental headquarters in Wuxi, who spoke to the two committee members about the circumstances of the 8th Company's pay being robbed, the two committee members immediately came to Chengcheng and sent a letter to the county government inquiring about the case's progress and handling. County Magistrate Li then ordered the Public Security Bureau to submit a report. The Public Security Bureau's report briefly stated that after receiving a phone call from the paymaster, who stated that Company Commander Wang had hired his rickshaw outside the South Gate and ordered him to pull to the North Gate, the rickshaw puller suddenly pulled to the East Gate, and the rickshaw puller's appearance and number were not remembered. Later, the bureau chief and the detective team, together with the garrison troops, surveyed the area outside the East Gate and encountered the paymaster, who stated that the company commander had originally gone to the North Gate and had arranged to send troops to the North Gate to wait, but unexpectedly he suddenly went to the East Gate. Someone on the boat inquired about the names of the company headquarters' buglers, etc. When being robbed, he saw a person in yellow clothes walk by for a few seconds, and then three or four people pushed the company commander into the field. The secret arrest of the robbers is currently underway, etc. Yesterday (the 29th), Committee Members Pan and Guo had already left Chengcheng. On the same day, after searching, suspects Zhou Fengyi, Zhu Lao San, Xu Shoulin, Zhou Juru, etc., were arrested and sent to the Public Security Bureau to be transferred to the county government for interrogation.

Investigation into Shi Chunsheng, who was Found to Be Suspicious: Wu Shanbao, a detective of the Public Security Bureau, and others, were recently ordered to investigate the case of Wang Tongfu and Bao Hansheng in Changjing Town, the 12th District. On the 28th, after Zhou Xiban's small steamer arrived at the port, Shi Chunsheng, who was found to be suspicious, was arrested. Two other people resembling soldiers or policemen took the opportunity to escape. He was sent to the district office. He claimed to have been sent by the Nanjing Special Municipal Party Department to investigate the case and showed a letter of commission issued by the Central Party Headquarters' Secretariat, following the Chairman's handwritten instructions. According to a secret report from Jiangyin citizens Cao Guocheng and Li Chuqing, Miao Chaoqun, who teaches at Changjing Junior High School in Qiaoqi Township, Cheng County, is a Communist Party member. Please arrest and investigate him. The letter of commission was issued by the Special Municipal Party Department using letterhead with an oval seal on June 18th and included two free train and boat travel permits, two business cards, and a book: "Military Magazine of the Central Military Academy, Lieutenant Secretary Shi Chunsheng, also known as Shufu, from Shaowu County, Fujian," and a book titled "Former Third Section Chief of Jiangyin County," etc. After arriving at the district office, Shi wrote three urgent letters in double-lined envelopes to the Special Municipal Party Department, Guo Jun and Huang Zhichen, etc., asking for help, and attached a letter to the Supreme Court, Ding Gongmao and Xiong Zheshen, asking Chen Qiuqi, the head of the Jiangyin Chamber of Commerce, and County Magistrate Li Leng to certify that it was not a fake municipal party committee member. It had already been sent to the post office, but the district office intercepted it, along with a letter to County Magistrate Li and a No. 26 badge from the Municipal Party Department. On the afternoon of the 29th, he was escorted to the Public Security Bureau by the Qincheng small steamer. At about 9:00 p.m., Bureau Chief Li interrogated him. According to Shi, he followed the Revolutionary Army in the Northern Expedition in the winter of the 15th year of the Republic (Headquarters of the 2nd Regiment, 1st Division, 14th Army) and arrived in Jiangsu. In February of the 16th year of the Republic, he arrived in Jiangyin. Because he had been wounded by bullets while attacking Jiangxi and had not yet recovered, he could no longer follow the army on its long journey. Therefore, he requested his regimental commander, Liao, to introduce him to the Jiangyin County Government and was reassigned to the Third Section as a section member. Later, County Magistrate Wang Guozuo appointed him as the director to temporarily take charge of the section's affairs. Later, he received a letter from home urging him to return home, so he returned to Fujian in May of the 16th year of the Republic. In the summer of the 18th year of the Republic, he was introduced by his teacher, Ding Boheng, who is now the Director of the Translation Section of the Military Magazine, to work as a secretary in the magazine. This June, he received a telegram from his elderly father at home (a native of Shaoxing, Zhejiang, who was appointed as the magistrate of Shaowu during the Qing Dynasty and stayed in Shaowu for twenty years) saying that the situation in Fujian was critical and urging him to return to Fujian as soon as possible to take care of family affairs. Therefore, he asked his superiors for leave to return home on June 18th and was approved and issued a travel permit. Unexpectedly, upon arriving in Shanghai, he heard that transportation in Fujian was blocked and that personnel from the Revolutionary Army entering Fujian were being subjected to increased scrutiny. Therefore, he did not dare to return home. Because the cost of living in Shanghai was too high and everything was expensive, it was not easy to live there. He then turned back. However, since he had already asked for leave, it was not convenient to return to the magazine immediately. A man from Changzhou named Li Zutai, with the courtesy name of Shuhua, had served as the director of the 8th District Tobacco and Alcohol Affairs Bureau in Shaowu ten years ago. His father had an eight-bow friendship with Li Zutai's father, and Li Zutai had taught him to write essays. Because of this relationship, he planned to temporarily rely on him. He would wait until Fujian was peaceful before returning home or transferring to the magazine to take up his duties. Unexpectedly, Li's address could not be found. He heard from the tea houses in the Changzhou hostel that Li seemed to be working in Changshu, but it was not confirmed. Helpless, he planned to come to Jiangyin to find his fellow villager Wu Chu because Wu had been stationed in Changshu and was familiar with the situation. Unfortunately, when he arrived in Jiangyin, Wu was not there. He had no choice but to stop here for a few days and did not visit any friends. He took a boat to Changshu on the 29th of the lunar calendar, but unexpectedly, Mr. Li was not there, so he made a wasted trip. Yesterday, he planned to return to Jiangyin and transfer to another place. However, on the way to Changjing, he suddenly suffered from an old illness and heart pain, so he temporarily wanted to rest in Changjing for a day before continuing his journey. When he arrived in Changjing, he stayed at a small inn. While wandering around on the way, he accidentally encountered Miao Chaoqun, a prostitute in Jiangyin who had a grudge against him. Miao Chaoqun greeted him. He secretly thought that the past feud had been forgotten after many years, so he had no choice but to exchange pleasantries with him. Miao insisted on providing him with food and lodging. Because he could not refuse, he went with Miao to his place. Unexpectedly, Miao harbored resentment and asked him, "You are a member of the military. You have come here alone after many years. Are you not a Communist Party detective?" He immediately stated that he was working at the Military Magazine of the National Revolutionary Army and had a passport as proof. He also said that he had often met with comrades from the Special Municipal Party Department in Nanjing. How could he be a Communist Party member? Moreover, Guo Jun, Huang Zhichen, and Zhang Shaoxian, three fellow villagers from the Special Municipal Party Department, had given him a badge from the Party Department so that he would not be mistaken for someone else on the road and could prove that he was a member of the Kuomintang. All of the above can be investigated. Unexpectedly, Miao, unable to harm him by calling him a Communist, used kind words to cover up his actions and insisted on keeping him in the school overnight. Because he wanted to explain his actions in Changjing, he was willing to stay there to show that he had not violated any laws. After dinner, he went out for a walk and returned to the school at 7:00 p.m. He did not see Miao return. After some time, the local defense corps and the detective team came to arrest him, etc. After the interrogation, he was detained and will be sent to the county government on the 30th for interrogation.

Rugao 93

Bandits Set Fire to Zhu Chen Village: On the night of the 25th, a group of bandits suddenly came to the home of Guo Anchen in Zhu Chen Village, south of Rugao City, armed with guns and breaking down the door. They first looted all the clothes, food, and other belongings, and then set fire to the entire house with kerosene and piled-up straw. Three main rooms were burned down, and all the furnishings were destroyed. Fortunately, the security corps stationed in Guo's mansion heard the alarm and led the team to the rescue, opening fire on the bandits, who then fled into the distance. Only the board walls and central pillars of the factory, hall, and side rooms were burned down, causing losses of no less than ten thousand yuan.

Bandits Rob Wealth and Extort Money: The family of Wu Zhengqing in Songjia Village, Dongchen District, is of modest means. On the night before last, dozens of bandits suddenly came and robbed them of more than 20 pieces of clothing and silver dollars. Before leaving, they severely beat the head of the household, causing serious injuries, and demanded that he raise 2,000 yuan within seven days, or else they would take appropriate measures.

Jiashan 94

Patrol Officer of Tao Village Accused of Negligence: Wu Qiwen, a resident of Xiadian Temple, accused Gao Zhiming, the patrol officer of the Tao Village branch station in Xitang, of dereliction of duty in violation of the law. The court has now approved the summons of witnesses to the case for a hearing on July 3 to investigate and interrogate.

The Head of the National Defense Corps Suspected of Colluding with Bandits Was Arrested: Xu, the head of the Jiashan City Defense Corps, and Ding, the instructor, are suspected of colluding with bandits and taking bribes. The volunteer defense corps arrested a bandit, A, the day before yesterday. A's interrogation confirmed the suspicions, so they swiftly arrested Xu and Ding. The incident caused a great uproar in the city for a time. Yesterday, the county government convened an emergency meeting of various agencies and organizations. The issue of disarming the defense corps was resolved through peaceful means. Ding was arrested, and Xu was temporarily released on bail, to be summoned at any time. All matters will be investigated for verification. It is said that they were falsely accused by bandits, but the truth is not yet known.

Pinghu 95

Bandits Captured in Quan Gong Pavilion: Since the local bandits in the east were severely suppressed by the military, their power has been collapsing. Recently, they gathered again in the area of Quan Gong Pavilion and Zhujia Dun, thinking of making trouble again. The Pinghu Camp headquarters learned of this and secretly ordered the 4th Company of the Provincial Security Team stationed in Xincang to encircle and suppress them. The company immediately surrounded and advanced from Sanyou River, Zhang Shu Tree, Zhujia Bridge, and other places. When they arrived at Quan Gong Pavilion, they saw five people dressed in a uniform manner resembling bandits in a certain tea house. When they saw the troops, they tried to escape. One person jumped into the river in an attempt to flee but was shot dead by the troops. Two others were shot on the spot and captured. It is reported that the names of the five people are Wu Zhenshi, Chen Jinlong Jiaozixiong, Tang Zhaohe, and Cai Arong.

Case of Forged Ginseng to be Interrogated Today: Tao Qinqiu, the owner of Jingyi Tang Pharmacy in this county, used fake ginseng worth 18 yuan to defraud Yan Acupuncture of Songfengtai of 240 yuan and forged the seals and invoices of a certain ginseng company in Shanghai. The Yan family discovered this and spread the word. The case was then learned by the pharmacy industry, who, out of concern for their reputation, filed a complaint with the county government. The county government has scheduled an interrogation for this afternoon.

A Person Died Under Economic Pressure: Ms. Chen, the owner of a certain shoe store on Ximen Street, was known for her virtue and kindness. Recently, because the store was unable to make a profit and expenses were high, coupled with the recent soaring rice prices, it was difficult to make a living. On the evening of the day before yesterday, she hanged herself upstairs. When her family discovered her, they rushed to call a Western doctor to treat her, but she had already died.

Hangzhou 96

Request to Send Commissioners to Survey the Provincial Border: The Zhejiang Provincial Government reported that disputes over the provincial border between Changhua and Xiuning counties on the border between Zhejiang and Anhui provinces have arisen repeatedly. Commissioner Wang Yongzhi was sent to conduct a survey. Now, it is learned that the authorities of the two provinces, Jiangsu and Zhejiang, have jointly requested the Ministry of Interior to send commissioners to conduct an on-site survey to facilitate administration.

Departure of the Southern Zhejiang Survey Team: The Zhejiang Construction Department presented a proposal to the Provincial Government meeting to organize a Southern Zhejiang Survey Team to understand the actual conditions of various places and lay the foundation for gradual construction in the future. The survey area of the team is divided into three regions: (1) the Ou River basin, (2) the coastal counties, and (3) the Qiantang River basin. The scope of the survey includes agriculture, geology, mineral resources, transportation, water conservancy, industry, and commerce. They are scheduled to depart from Hangzhou on the 1st and will be limited to three months.

Shangyu 97

The Chunhui Middle School Bandit Case: It has been half a month since the Chunhui Middle School bandit case occurred. The three kidnapped people are still in danger. Principal Fan Shoukang and teacher Wu Minxing recently sent letters to their families from the bandit's den, detailing their various difficulties. Fan Shoukang's father, Fan Gaoping, came south from Yingkou after hearing the news to try to rescue his son. The bandits believe that Fan Gaoping has been doing business in the north for many years and must have a lot of wealth. Therefore, they have very high expectations. In fact, Fan has suffered repeated business failures in recent years due to the current situation, and he is naturally generous and enthusiastic about public welfare and has no savings. Even if he wants to prepare money for redemption, it will be difficult. Therefore, it is still unknown whether his beloved son can be rescued. The reporter visited Fan yesterday to inquire about the recent situation. Fan replied that he had incurred a great deal of debt before the 15th year of the Republic, which his relatives and friends knew. He only made a small profit after operating a refined salt company starting in the 16th year of the Republic and gradually paid off his old debts. Although he has gained some reputation in recent years, the only things that can be called assets are various stocks such as Jiudali Yuan, with a face value of only 40,000 to 50,000 yuan. Last year, due to business failure, he mortgaged a portion of the stocks to the Coal Industry Zhengli and Liang Banks for 20,000 yuan. Moreover, he has always advocated the abolition of inheritance and responded to the request of the local education community years ago to designate 20,000 yuan as an education fund. The remainder is for his own retirement needs, which is still not enough. Now that his beloved son has suffered this unexpected disaster, he will of course do his best to rescue him, but if the rescue costs are beyond his ability, he can only listen to fate. Educational News.

Important News 98

Educational Expenses Statistics for Anhui Province in the 18th Year of the Republic

Totaling over 1.92 Million Yuan

An Increase of Approximately 500,000 Yuan Compared to the Previous Year

The local education funding in Anhui Province has been extremely strained. Since Director Cheng took office, he has implemented a cleanup of the education funding in various counties and has made great efforts to increase funding. Over the past year, the total amount of education funding in various counties has increased significantly compared to before. According to the latest statistics from the compilation office of the Education Department, the total amount of education funding in 60 counties in the province in the 18th year of the Republic was 1,921,771 yuan, an increase of approximately 500,000 yuan compared to the total amount in the 17th year of the Republic (the total amount of education funding in 60 counties in the 17th year of the Republic was 1,440,829 yuan). The number of educational expenses in 60 counties in Anhui Province in the 18th year of the Republic is summarized below:

Municipal Primary Schools 99

Joint Graduation Ceremony

Continuing to Hold Primary School Concert

The Shanghai Municipal Primary School Joint Graduation Ceremony, hosted by the Municipal Education Bureau, was held at the Zhabei Renewal Stage at 9:00 a.m. yesterday. More than 2,500 graduates from various schools attended. Director Chen, the chairman, performed the ceremony as usual.

Director's Speech: Today is the first joint graduation ceremony of Shanghai Municipal Primary Schools. There have been two joint ceremonies in the past, but only municipal schools were included. Private schools that were registered were not included. This year, registered private schools that participated in the joint examination have joined, so this can be said to be the joint graduation ceremony of all primary schools in Shanghai. The graduates this time faced more difficulties than before because they had to pass the joint examination to graduate. In the past, the power to decide whether or not to graduate rested with the head of the school, and often due to the considerable feelings between teachers and students, students with relatively poor grades were also allowed to graduate. I believe that primary school students are the foundation of all schools. Whether or not they can achieve great things and become good citizens in the future depends on their primary school years. Therefore, primary schools should be taken seriously. If grades are not good, but graduation is allowed due to personal feelings, it will have a great impact on the country and the nation in the future. Therefore, the joint examination is used to determine whether or not to graduate. Many of those who participated in the examination but failed to graduate are not necessarily worse than those who graduated, but those who graduated have paid considerable attention to their studies and are able to enjoy today's honor. After graduation, they will either work or continue their studies. You should all know that your knowledge is too little and your existing knowledge is not enough to apply. Whether you continue your studies or not, you must continue to work hard after graduation. Everything in the world is learning, and everyone in the world except me is my teacher. Therefore, you must study everywhere in society and pay attention at all times, and you will surely achieve considerable success in the future. I am very happy today that everyone has a good attitude and can maintain order. I hope that everyone will always maintain this good attitude and the good habit of maintaining order. You will naturally be a good citizen in society in the future. At the same time, let others see you and want to learn to be a good citizen. After the ceremony, there will be a concert. On the one hand, it will make us happy, and on the other hand, it will cultivate our character. Don't forget this memorable June 30th, my words, and your good attitude and order today.

Mayor's Speech: Secretary Cen Dezhang delivered the speech on behalf of the Mayor. This graduation ceremony used the method of joint examination. Before the examination, the municipal government and the education bureau felt that the level of Shanghai's municipal and private primary schools was uneven, and the quality of education varied. Therefore, the idea of a joint examination was proposed. After the examination, according to Director Chen's report, the level was indeed uneven. The uneven level has an impact on teaching materials and teachers. In particular, it has suppressed many talented and good students. The classmates who participated in this graduation ceremony are naturally very honored. I hope you will tell the classmates who failed the examination that failure is the mother of success, and that if you work hard again, you will surely graduate next year. In particular, I hope that those who graduated will not be arrogant and think that passing the joint examination is just the best stage of your life. There will be many difficult examinations to enter middle school and university in the future. Finally, I offer three key points for everyone, whether you continue your studies or work in the future: (1) what, (2) how to seek, and (3) why to seek. Maintaining this attitude at all times will bring great progress.

Speech by the Representative of the Party Department: Huang Zaoxiong delivered a speech and briefly reported on a point of view. China has two difficult problems to solve: (1) There are too many Chinese people with shallow knowledge. In other words, there are still many people who have not received primary school education. Today, all of you have received this primary school education and graduated. From today onwards, China will have another group of knowledgeable citizens. I hope that everyone will become a good, knowledgeable citizen who has received primary school education. (2) There is a lack of talented people with advanced knowledge in Chinese society. To have advanced knowledge, you must obtain advanced education. Therefore, I hope that everyone will continue to seek advanced knowledge, from primary school to middle school to university to graduate school, so that China can add many more talented people with advanced knowledge who are needed by society.

Speech by the Representative of the Principals: Wu Bokang, the principal of Wanzhu School, delivered a speech. This joint graduation ceremony is more grand than the previous two because this time it comes from a joint examination, so this graduation is also more accurate. Many of you children will no longer pursue further studies from now on, and many will continue their studies. Bokang, on behalf of the principals, has a few words to tell you. To the children who do not enter school, you must still be careful and learn knowledge and skills everywhere. The school only leads you to the door. From now on, it will be the opening of your career. There are many things in society that you can research and discuss, as long as you are willing to be careful. Among the children who continue their studies in middle school, there is a bad habit. Now, there are many reactionary elements who use a theory to lure young people. The teachers in primary school manage strictly, but middle school is different. You must always pay attention and not be tempted by others. Many good young people are very good in primary school, but later they are led astray by others. I hope everyone will pay attention.

Municipal Administration Expert 103

Mr. Yuan Xiamin is about to return to China. Mr. Yuan Xiamin is from Fengxin, Jiangxi, and is 28 years old this year. He graduated from Yuzhang Middle School and Tongwen College in Jiangxi. In the spring of the 13th year of the Republic of China, he went to the United States at his own expense to study at Bowling Green State University, majoring in sociology and municipal administration, and obtained seven degrees. He then entered Columbia University to major in

municipal administration and obtained a master's degree. Therefore, he has profound research and insights in municipal administration. Lehua Sports Association Hosts 113

Chinese Expedition Soccer Team Sets Sail Today at 2:00 PM at the New Bund Wharf

The Chinese Amateur Soccer Team, hosted by the Lehua Sports Association in 1930, which has been rumored for a long time, set sail on the British ship Kanmalo at 2:30 PM today at the New Bund Wharf. They will first go to Hong Kong and then to Singapore for several matches. Then, on August 22nd, they will go to Europe. It is expected to last about eight months and will have more than 40 matches. This trip is still an unprecedented initiative. The purpose is to promote the spirit of sports in our country and to learn from others and correct our mistakes. It is also extremely relevant to international honor. The details are recorded below.

Motivation for Expedition to Europe and America 114

Yu Hengzhi, the leader of the team, once said that the motivation for the Chinese expedition to Europe and America was as early as four years ago. At that time, he had this ideal and cultivated Lehua talents year by year to improve their level. Now that the time is ripe, it has become a reality, and I am secretly comforted. However, the shame of the Far East Games, where Japan and China drew, also made Yu have to make a determination to prepare for the promotion of national prestige in the future.

Selection of the Expeditionary Force 115

The Chinese expedition soccer team this time is organized by the Lehua Sports Association. The selection of players is extremely cautious. They must first be selected by the directors of the association before the association can contact them separately. The goal is not only to have superior skills, but also to have good character. The purpose of this expedition is to not only improve skills and improve the level, but also to be a representative of Chinese new youth. They must show the spirit of great citizens everywhere.

List of Expeditionary Force Members 116

Leader and Secretary: Yu Hengzhi, Captain: Li Huitang, Doctor: Guan Jianan, Treasurer: Li Silian, Team Members: Zhou Xianyan, Dai Linjing, Li Ning, Feng Yunyou, Chen Zhenhe, Sun Sijing, Chen Jiaqiu, An Yuansheng (above are from Shanghai), Li Tiansheng, Cao Guicheng, Ye Beihua, Chen Guangyao, Feng Jingxiang, Wu Jinquan (above are from Guangdong), Bao Jiaping is also being recruited, but it has not been determined. There are also three people selected in Singapore and Java. If they cannot be found, a telegram will be sent to the country to recruit them. In total, there are 18 players, plus the leader, doctor, and treasurer, totaling 21 people.

Funding is not a Problem 117

The funding for the expedition has been sponsored by sports enthusiasts and does not seem to be a problem. In case of a shortfall, efforts will be made to raise funds during the competition in Java. As for the amount of sponsorship, the leader Yu Hengzhi is not convenient to announce it because the donors do not want to be publicized. As for the surplus of more than 6,000 yuan from the previous southern expedition, more than 5,000 yuan has been used last year, and there is not much left. In addition, the team only received 400 yuan in travel expenses from the Association during the last soccer season, and the rest was supplemented by the team, so the cost was very high.

Li Huitang Went to Singapore Last Month 118

Captain Li Huitang went to Hong Kong in mid-last month and then arrived in Singapore to negotiate the matches in Singapore and Java. It has been agreed to have two matches in Singapore and twelve matches in Java. The funds for going to Europe depend entirely on the income from ticket sales for several matches.

First Go to Hong Kong and then to Singapore 119

They will depart today and arrive in Hong Kong around the 4th. They will immediately go ashore to practice and take the original ship to Singapore on the 5th. They can arrive in that port on the 9th. On July 13th, they will play their first match against the Malayan Chinese team. On the 16th, they will play against the Singapore European team, for a total of two matches.

Go to Java for the Match 120

After playing two matches in Singapore, they will go to Java from Singapore on July 18th. It is expected to arrive on the 20th and stay for a month, with a total of about 12 matches to raise funds for going to Europe. They will leave Java on August 18th and return to Singapore. The order of matches in Java is as follows: Match Date, Location, and Team Name: July 22nd, Bandung vs. Bandung Players, July 24th, Bandung vs. Bandung League Champion, July 26th, Batavia vs. Ikulas, July 27th, Batavia vs. Batavia Players, July 30th, Longchuan vs. Longchuan Players Team, August 1st, Longchuan vs. Java Players Team or Longchuan League Champion August 3rd, Surabaya vs. Surabaya Players Team, August 5th, Surabaya vs. Tol or Essexiu, August 7th, Surabaya vs. Chinese Football Team, August 10th, Batavia vs. Ministry of Internal Affairs, August 13th, Batavia vs. Qunli Team, August 17th, Batavia vs. All-Java Players.

Go to Europe from Singapore 121

After the battles in Singapore and Java, they will take the Rajpurana ship from Singapore on August 22nd to Europe, arriving in Marseille, France on September 12th, and then to Austria, Hungary, and Germany. The itinerary after that has not yet been determined. It is expected to arrive in the UK in early November and return to China in late January next year after arriving in Canada and the United States. There will be about 30 to 34 matches in Europe.

Harris Goes to Europe to Negotiate 122

This expedition has been brewing for a long time. It was said last winter that Harris, a British businessman in Shanghai, took advantage of his trip to the UK and entrusted Harris to negotiate matches with various European countries. According to Harris's telegram, Austria, Hungary, and Germany have made firm decisions, and the rest are still in negotiation.

Li Silian Departs Next Month 123

The Englishman Li Silian has lived in Shanghai for more than ten years and has a good relationship with the Chinese sports community. Mr. Li returned to China last year and also helped to negotiate the order of the expedition. When Mr. Li returned to Shanghai, he served as the director of Weile Garden. The Chinese team's expedition benefited a lot from Mr. Li, so Mr. Li was invited to be responsible for managing the economy and taking care of everything along the way. Mr. Li will not travel with the expeditionary force and will go directly to Singapore on August 12th and then go to Europe together.

Three Strong Players Have Gone to Singapore 124

The Hong Kong strong players Li Tiansheng, Ye Beihua, and Feng Jingxiang are important members of the expeditionary force. The three gentlemen had already gone to Singapore on June 22nd.

Future Activities of Lehua 125

The reputation of the Lehua team in Shanghai has always been praised by Chinese and Westerners. Now that the entire team's elite has embarked on an expedition to Europe and America, whether Lehua can still present its active phenomenon in the Shanghai soccer community as in the past is of concern to all Shanghai people. According to Mr. Yu Hengzhi, during the eight-month period when the team is away from the country, the activities of the Lehua Sports Association in Shanghai have been entrusted to Mr. Wu Bangwei and Mr. Wang Fudan. Therefore, in the future, the banner of the Lehua soccer team in Western soccer associations will still be able to be displayed in front of the audience.

Recruitment of Sports Talents 128

National Jinan University has always been famous at home and abroad for its expertise in sports. Recently, a well-known middle school in Jiangsu Province has extended an invitation to a sports teacher from the school to serve as a track and field coach and ball sports instructor, and to teach general gymnastics for about 16 hours per week. The treatment is generous (more than 100 yuan per month). Among the school's graduates in the past, there is no shortage of talents to choose from, but they all want to show their skills again in the next Far East Games and win glory for the country. If they accept this appointment, they will inevitably lose their amateur qualifications. The school's sports major is still in preparation, so for the time being, it has to find sports teachers from other schools to find a qualified person with a degree in sports from a national or registered private university, or a graduate of a sports major with high skills and rich teaching experience, or a graduate of a university with special research in sports who has a considerable position in previous sports meets. If you wish to apply, you can send a detailed resume and a letter of introduction from your alma mater directly to "Mr. Li Bangdong, Jinan University, Zhenru." After strict review and evaluation, if you are deemed qualified, you will be notified of the appointment.

North Szechuan Road, Yu Qing Fang 130

Negotiations Regarding Water Supply – Residents Suffer from Water Shortage During the Scorching Summer – Three Bureaus Dispatch Personnel to Provide Relief – Yu Qing Fang on North Szechuan Road consists of 186 buildings. Facing North Szechuan Road, there is only one alley entrance; facing Changchun Road, there are five alley entrances. The property belongs to Li Jigao, and it has been using the concession's water and electricity. During the arrival of the Revolutionary Army in Shanghai in the 16th year of the Republic of China, the owner actually bricked up the five alley entrances leading to Changchun Road and requested the Public Concession’s Public Works Department (工部局) police to guard the North Szechuan Road alley entrance. Unexpectedly, the Public Works Department used this as an excuse to forcibly collect police fees from the tenants. Those tenants who resisted had their electricity cut off by the Public Works Department. The tenants were greatly angered and appealed to the former Jiangsu Bureau of Foreign Affairs (江蘇交涉公署), which questioned the Public Works Department. The Public Works Department replied that anyone using the concession's water and electricity should pay the concession police fees. If the Chinese area could supply water and electricity, the fees would not be collected, etc. Upon hearing this, the tenants first broke open two of the bricked-up rear doors and requested the municipal government to station police in the neighborhood for protection, and also requested that the connection to Chinese area water and electricity be expedited. The Public Utilities Bureau (公用局) complied with the unanimous request of the residents and immediately arranged for the installation of water pipes and electric wires. On September 19th of the 17th year of the Republic of China, they, together with the Public Works and Public Safety Bureaus, sent a letter to the property owner requesting them to voluntarily switch over to Chinese area water and electricity. The letter was delivered by the district police to the rental accounting firm. Unexpectedly, both the rental foreign firm and the property owner's residence claimed that the property owner was not in Shanghai and refused to accept it. Subsequently, on October 11th of the 18th year of the Republic of China, the Public Utilities Bureau issued a notice prohibiting residents in the Chinese-concession boundary area from arbitrarily using the concession's water and electricity. Those who had already connected to the concession's water and electricity should immediately switch to Chinese area water and electricity. However, the property owner of the Yu Qing Fang still ignored it. On March 10th of the 19th year of the Republic of China, the Shanghai Waterworks Company (上海自來水公司) planned to move the water meter originally located at the Changchun Road entrance to the North Szechuan Road entrance, and submitted a road excavation permit request to the Public Utilities Bureau. The bureau deemed this action to be completely unreasonable and denied the request. However, several days later, the company arbitrarily started excavating the road on the North Szechuan Road sidewalk, cut off the pipes, and installed the meter. The residents of Yu Qing Fang, due to the sudden interruption of water supply, requested relief from the Fifth Branch, First Precinct of the Public Safety Bureau (公安局五區一所). The branch dispatched police to persuade them to stop work and restore the water supply. Last Saturday (June 28th), at 2:00 PM, the Public Utilities Bureau suddenly received a letter from the Public Concession’s Public Works Department, stating that they would start work on installing water pipes in front of Yu Qing Fang starting at 8:00 AM this Monday (yesterday), and claiming that the North Szechuan Road sidewalk belonged to the Public Works Department, requesting that the district police be notified not to interfere, etc. At the same time, the Public Works and Public Safety Bureaus also received the same notice. After consultation among the three bureaus, it was believed that although the water meter was located on the sidewalk, the water pipes entered Yu Qing Fang, which was located in the Chinese area. The Public Works Department's approval of the Shanghai Waterworks Company to cut and install the water meter without the consent of the municipal government was simply allowing the water company to defy the municipal laws. The only way to resist was to cut off the water pipes inside the alley. However, by then it was past the Public Works Department's office hours and there was no way to contact them. They immediately sent a letter via express mail, declaring that they did not recognize this illegal action and hoped that they would cease the operation. At the same time, the Public Safety Bureau notified the Dixwell Road Police Station (狄思威路捕房) by telephone to relay this matter to the directors of the Public Works Department. However, according to the police chief, this matter was entirely the initiative of Mr. Haas, the director of the Public Works Department, who was currently out and could not be contacted. The Public Utilities Bureau, not receiving a satisfactory response, and to prepare for any eventuality, dispatched personnel on Sunday to inform the district precinct and the residents' association of Yu Qing Fang, requesting them to inform the residents to store more water in the evening so that if the Shanghai Waterworks Company shut off the water supply during the installation of the meter the next day, they would have a reserve in case of the heavy water usage during the hot summer. Yesterday, the bureau, together with the Public Works and Public Safety Bureaus, dispatched personnel to Yu Qing Fang at 7:00 AM to observe any actions. At 9:00 AM, the police chief of the Dixwell Road Police Station arrived with seven or eight armed police officers and many workers from the Shanghai Waterworks Company. They first closed the water valve to prepare to cut the pipes and install the meter. Personnel dispatched by the Public Utilities Bureau immediately went forward and politely advised them, saying that the municipal government had a solution and had notified the Public Works Department, and that it would not be too late to take action after receiving a reply from the Public Works Department. However, because the police chief and others were adamant in their views, they could only listen. However, in order to implement the planned measures, they hired workers from the Cleanliness Company (潔麗公司). After they cut off the water pipe under the sidewalk, they also cut off the water pipes inside the alley. At that time, it was exactly 11:00 AM, and the residents were using a lot of water. The public bathhouses (老虎灶) in the area could not meet the demand, and eventually there was not a drop of water left. Preparing to seek help, the personnel dispatched by the Public Utilities Bureau believed that this kind of water shortage in the summer would be detrimental to public safety and sanitation. They immediately notified the Zhabei Water and Electricity Company (閘北水電公司) to send workers to open all of the Taiping Faucets (太平龍頭) along Changchun Road for the residents to use for emergency needs, and also connected the water pipes inside Yu Qing Fang to the Chinese area water pipes on Changchun Road. The installation was completed at 5:00 PM, and water supply was continued. If the property owner could negotiate with the Zhabei Water and Electricity Company and switch to their water and electricity, then this case could be resolved from then on.

Municipal Chamber of Commerce 131

Executive and Supervisory Committee Takes Office Today

Commercial Reorganization Committee Submits Report of Cancellation – The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce's Executive and Supervisory Committee members, after being elected by the citywide representatives' congress according to law, immediately convened a discussion meeting and decided to hold a swearing-in ceremony for all Executive and Supervisory Committee members at 9:00 AM today. The Ministry of Industry and Commerce and the municipal party and government organs have been invited to dispatch personnel to deliver instructions. After taking office, the first Executive Committee meeting will be held to elect standing committee members and elect a chairman to handle the handover matters. The telegram from the Ministry of Industry and Commerce and the telegram from the Commercial Reorganization Committee reporting the cancellation are recorded below:

Telegram from the Ministry of Industry and Commerce to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce: Your report has been received. Director Zhao Xien, Assistant Shou Jingwei, and Clerk Jingwei have been dispatched to represent the Ministry and deliver instructions at the designated time. Please take note and apply to the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau to dispatch personnel to supervise the election in accordance with Article 14 of the Implementing Regulations of the Chamber of Commerce Law. [Signed] Ministry of Industry and Commerce, Qian.

Report from the Commercial Reorganization Committee: The Commercial Reorganization Committee has yesterday reported to the Central Party Headquarters, the National Government, the Ministry of Industry and Commerce in Nanjing, and sent separate letters to the Municipal Party Headquarters, the Civil Education Committee, and the Municipal Government's Social Affairs Bureau, stating that Article 15 of the Organizational Outline of Associations stipulates that the Shanghai Commercial Reorganization Committee should be abolished after the promulgation of unified association organizational laws and the establishment of unified association organizations. Now that the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce has been established in accordance with the Chamber of Commerce Law, all newly elected officials of the association will take office on July 1st, and all association duties will be transferred to the chamber for handling from this day forward. The official seal used by the association was issued by your ministry and should be returned on this day. However, since the seal issued to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce by the Ministry of Industry and Commerce will take some time to arrive, the association may temporarily need to borrow it for official documents. The Municipal Chamber of Commerce will submit a separate document in the future. The Shanghai Special Municipality Commercial Group Reorganization Committee respectfully reports that the Municipal Chamber of Commerce has been established, the association has been abolished in accordance with regulations from this day forward, and the situation is reported to your ministry for review and record, for the sake of public convenience.

French Concession 132

Labor Strike at Water and Electricity Company – Company Issues Notice – The French Concession Water and Electricity Company posted its fourth notice yesterday, stating that since the labor strike occurred on the 18th, there have been many inconveniences for customers, and they deeply apologize. They have decided to recruit new workers and resume work starting on July 1st, which is hereby announced.

Trade Union Meeting – The trade union reopened a members' meeting at the public sports field outside Ximen at 3:00 PM yesterday. More than 400 workers attended, all wearing union badges. Xu Yefu from the Municipal Civil Education Committee attended to provide guidance. Chief Inspector Gao from the Second Precinct of the Municipal Public Safety Bureau led many police officers to patrol the field. The meeting was held under the scorching sun for two hours. After the meeting, the attendees lined up and dispersed at the trade union. The approved motions and the remarks of the representative of the Municipal Civil Education Committee are briefly recorded below:

Approved Motions – First, Chairman Xu Amei reported on the company's recent notice and the arrest of two workers by the French police and one worker by the Second Precinct of the Public Safety Bureau the day before yesterday, and asked all workers to discuss the countermeasures. It was unanimously resolved that regarding the arrested workers, a petition should be submitted to the Municipal Party Headquarters and the Social Affairs Bureau, and a letter should be sent to Du Yuesheng, a Chinese director in the French Concession, to forward to the French police, requesting their release within two days. Regarding the company's notice of recruiting new workers, all workers should investigate at any time whether any new workers have entered the factory and report to the trade union. It was decided that another members' meeting would be held the day after tomorrow (Wednesday) to discuss countermeasures.

Party Headquarters Remarks – Xu Yefu from the Municipal Civil Education Committee made remarks stating that he has represented the Municipal Party Headquarters at your meetings more than once, but today he does not feel very happy because some of the workers in your union cannot absolutely obey the discipline of the strike committee, resulting in conflicts with the workers in the vehicle department in the past two days. It must be known that the reason why the vehicle workers cannot fight on the same front is because of the timing and circumstances, and we must not obstruct traffic because of momentary impatience. Therefore, he hopes that all workers will unite and fight together under the leadership of the Chinese Kuomintang, and especially pay attention to strike discipline and not take any actions that go beyond the bounds, so that they will surely win the final victory.

Yesterday's Dispute – Yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM, all the workers were marching in an orderly fashion from the trade union on Luban Road to the public sports field in the east to hold a meeting. When passing the intersection of Xieqiao Linin Road, a French Concession Route 6 streetcar, No. 18, was coming from the north and drove into the Chinese area. Because the driver sped up the car in an attempt to scatter the workers, the crowd on the road and some of the workers were extremely indignant and went forward to argue with the driver, but it was ineffective, which led to a conflict. Several pieces of glass on the car were broken. The police on duty rushed to suppress the situation, and the ticket seller Liu Bingting and the cart pusher Wang Xinbao were injured by stones and sent to Guangci Hospital on Jinshenfu Road by Chief Inspector Gao of the Second Precinct of the Municipal Public Safety Bureau. It was heard that one of the workers, Zhu Guangde, had his leg hit by the car at the time.

Foreign Silver Imports Disappear 133

The main reason for the drastic fall in silver prices is the excessive import of foreign silver, which has led to supply exceeding demand, resulting in a daily increase in silver reserves and a drastic fall in prices. Since the customs authorities ordered the prohibition of foreign silver imports, Hong Kong still allows imports, so the source of foreign silver has not been completely eliminated. Last week, Hong Kong also banned the import of silver dollars, and this port has also intensified the crackdown, so those engaged in this business have no way to smuggle them in, and as a result, they have disappeared. According to a survey yesterday, not a trace of foreign silver or silver dollars were imported in the past week. The total number of silver ingots transported from this port to other ports such as Hangzhou, Hong Kong, and Mumbai is estimated to be more than 2,070, so the amount of silver reserves in this port is decreasing day by day.

Gold Bar Shipments to the United States Statistics – Total for May – According to the United States Consulate General in Shanghai yesterday, the total value of gold bars and cash exported from China (including Hong Kong) to the United States in May totaled US$434,351. The total from January to May of this year is US$9,833,105.

Low-Priced Rice 135

Sold at a Low Price of Three Yuan per Shi – Actively Continuing to Raise Funds – Preparing for Losses in Low-Priced Rice – The Municipal Rice Price Stabilization Committee, due to the recent tension in the rice market, held its sixth meeting at the Social Affairs Bureau at 2:00 PM on June 26th. The attending committee members included Yao Zirang, Zhu Zixiang, Yan Xiaoquan, Cai Yukun, Wang Boxun, Xu Fu (represented by Xu Fengzao), Tang Naikang (represented by Zhang Yinhuai), Mo Zijing, Gu Xinyi, Lu Wenshao, Fan Hesheng, Huang Hanzhi, Pan Gongzhan, and more than ten other people. Committee Chairman Pan presided over the meeting. The following are the important resolutions of the meeting: (1) As rice prices rise and sales of low-priced rice increase sharply, the committee's rice reserves are running low. How should we find ways to maintain the supply? It was resolved to adopt two measures: 1. The purchasing committee members should first contact rice merchants. If the current rice stock is sold out and new rice cannot be supplied, the rice should be borrowed from the merchants and returned as soon as the goods arrive. 2. As fundraising is difficult, the low-priced rice is priced too far below market prices, which will be difficult to sustain. It was resolved that the selling price will be set at 450 copper coins per sheng starting on July 1st, which is still more than three yuan per shi lower than the market price. The Social Affairs Bureau will issue a public notice. (2) Donations have not been enthusiastic, which has made the advance payments difficult. How should we quickly raise funds? It was resolved that the committee should send a letter to the Miscellaneous Grain Association to be responsible for raising donations for low-priced rice, with a minimum of 10,000 yuan. Committee members Ye Huijun and Cai Yukun will be responsible for raising 5,000 yuan to cover the shortfall in the Jiagutang. Committee member Lu Wenshao will allocate 5,000 yuan from the Money Trade Association within this week. Committee member Wang Boxun will ask Mr. Qin Runqing to help raise 20,000 yuan from the Banking Association. The committee will send personnel to collect the funds and the committee members will conduct fundraising from all sectors.

Tianjin Allows Flexible Pickup of Goods 136

Pickup Based on Tax Receipts – Yesterday, the shipping companies in this port formally received a telegram from Tianjin stating that the Tianjin Customs will no longer insist on the payment of supplementary taxes for goods shipped from Shanghai for which the import half-tax has already been paid in Shanghai. The flexible measure has also been announced. It is only necessary to send the red receipt for the shipped goods with the vessel and submit the Tianjin Customs half-tax receipt that has been paid to the Jianghai Customs for verification. If it is deemed to be correct, the customers will be allowed to pick up the goods.

Chinese Vessels Temporarily Maintain Transportation – The Chinese vessels in this port originally planned to suspend sailings to Tianjin starting on July 1st to avoid losses from empty voyages. Yesterday, a telegram was received from Tianjin stating that goods from Shanghai will be allowed to be picked up with flexibility, and the Beiyang Gang requested that sailings be maintained as usual to maintain freight transport. Therefore, the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Xinfeng vessel and others will still sail on the Shanghai-Tianjin route today.

Municipal Social Affairs Bureau Purchases Rice Stem Borer Eggs 146

Temporary Purchasing Stations Established in Wusong, Jiangwan, and Yinhang Districts – In order to encourage farmers in the city to make efforts to search and kill rice stem borer eggs and moths, the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau recently submitted a request to the Municipal Government to allocate temporary funds to establish purchasing stations in the municipal committee's office in Wusong, Jiangwan, and Yinhang districts first. Afterwards, the scope of expansion will be determined based on the severity of rice stem borer damage and the situation of purchasing rice stem borer eggs and moths. It is heard that the bureau has decided to dispatch personnel to start purchasing in the respective areas on the 2nd of this month. The purchasing methods are recorded below:

Shanghai Municipal Social Affairs Bureau's Methods for Purchasing Rice Stem Borer Eggs (1) The bureau will establish purchasing stations in areas with severe rice stem borer damage in the city to purchase rice stem borer eggs and moths for the purpose of preventing and eliminating rice stem borer damage. (2) The bureau's purchasing stations will be temporarily established in Wusong, Jiangwan, and Yinhang districts first. (3) Each purchasing station will have a director, who will be concurrently held by the municipal committee member of the respective district, and will be responsible for all affairs of the station. The purchasing staff will be concurrently filled by the staff of the municipal committee's office, and will be given a monthly allowance of eight yuan. (4) The purchasing stations will be under the guidance and supervision of the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau. (5) The purchased rice stem borer eggs and moths should be submitted to the Social Affairs Bureau for verification and cancellation before 2:00 PM every Monday. (6) Farmers should first tie ten egg masses into a bundle and ten moths into a bag when selling rice stem borer eggs and moths. (7) The purchase price will be temporarily set at one copper coin for each rice stem borer egg and one copper coin for every two rice stem borer moths at the beginning. (8) The purchase time will be set from 8:00 AM to 4:00 PM every day. (9) The purchase period will be temporarily set for the months of July and August.

Sino-Japanese Nanjing Incident Loss Negotiations 147

Japanese Residents Cannot Provide Evidence? – The Office of the Japanese Consulate in Shanghai has repeatedly received reports from Japanese residents' associations in Nanjing and Shanghai inquiring about the progress of the negotiations of the Nanjing Incident Loss Investigation Committee and the date of its resolution. Commissioner Shimizu and lawyer Murakami, who are handling this case, are both in Shanghai. Yesterday, Chargé d'Affaires Shigemitsu convened the commissioners to inquire about everything. Currently, because the commissioners from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs are insisting on justice, the amount of losses claimed by the Japanese side is too large and lacks standards, and they must provide solid evidence. However, the Japanese commissioners claim that the Japanese residents were caught off guard at the time of the incident, and there was no way to collect evidence of losses afterwards. The only way to resolve the issue is for the Japanese commissioners to voluntarily reduce the amount of compensation for the Nanjing Incident losses, which may lead to an earlier resolution. Chargé d'Affaires Shigemitsu has already telegraphed the Japanese government for instructions.
