American Five-Year-Old Composer 215

Although only five years old, Patricia Anne Sampson of Cedar Falls, Iowa, USA, has attracted the attention of the entire city because she is already able to compose piano music. Patricia is the daughter of a piano professor at the Provincial Normal College. Like the famous Mozart, she was able to play the piano when most children were too young to show any musical talent. She has never received any formal instruction from her father, G.W. Sampson, Jr. She has already composed half a dozen pieces without any intention of guiding her, but her abilities have fully developed. A waltz called "Peter Pan" is her favorite, and everyone who has heard the piece also loves it. Randolph Ganz, the president of the Chicago Conservatory of Music, after hearing her work, advised, "It is best to let her develop her talent freely." When she was only two years old, she would climb onto the piano keys whenever she had the chance. After that, she began to amaze her parents because she was able to play the pieces that she usually heard her father teach his students. Among these pieces are Bohm's "The Fountain," Heller's "Curious Story," Von's "The Infant Jesus," and Paderewski's "Melody in B." A visitor who came to their home sang her a song called "Bye Baby Byelo," and she immediately sang along. She could sing and play everything that her parents sang and played for her when she was asleep. Abo Freeman, another piano professor at the Normal College, said, "What people have to learn has already been born with her. She will become a special composer and pianist." In addition to the piano, she still likes to play with dolls and dogs (Kewpies) like other children.

Dedicated to Young People Who Love Literature and Art 216

Ji Ping

From a psychological perspective, we can see that youth is the most intense period of life. Not only are there significant physical developments, but also a leap in psychological characteristics. Emotions at this stage are no longer as easily extinguished or limited to the present scope and trivial matters. With the expansion of the world and the development of knowledge, emotions are more persistent and demand concrete expression. This demand is reflected in the emergence of love and attention to social causes. At the same time, a love of literature and art is a common and powerful tendency during this period. Because literature and art are originally the organization of emotions, it is only natural that this path is most suitable for young people with rich emotions. Looking at the literary history of various countries, almost every writer started working hard in their youth, and some even became famous in their youth. What does this fact illustrate? It is that the combination of youth and literature and art is by no means accidental but has a strong psychological foundation.

Picture of a Painter Pon Hsün Ch’ing (Shot by Hsü Wei Nan) 217

At the same time, it also has social significance. We know that literature and art are part of culture, and culture is a product of the nation. Youth is a group with creative abilities, the vanguard of the era, and the main force of the nation. Therefore, in the sense of popularizing and improving culture, in other words, in promoting the glory of the nation, youth is inevitably endowed with this mission, and the pursuit of literary and artistic work is the practice of this mission. In short, youth and literature and art should become a purposeful combination, that is, on the one hand, based on the inherent artistic requirements, and at the same time, not standing on a personal standpoint but taking national culture as a prerequisite for conscious action.

Chinese youth, in the past years, groaned under autocracy like other people, and almost lost the characteristics that youth should have. Literature and art were forgotten. The so-called scholars only revolved around the fantasy of promotion. This was determined by objective historical conditions, and we don't need to blame them. However, after the Xinhai Revolution, the tumultuous May Fourth Movement followed. This movement evolved from politics to culture, and the cultural movement was mainly focused on literary revolution. Originally, this movement was created by young students. By this time, young people in general were deeply connected with literature and art. We can see from the works of that time and everything else that young people had a crazy enthusiasm for literature and art. This enthusiasm laid the foundation for the new literature in general. After that, with the evolution of society, the May Fourth Movement was divided into water and less youth. The efforts of young people in literature and art have also become several forces, each boasting of its own literary and artistic group. When the National Revolutionary Army marched north and the military power reached the Yangtze River, many young people immersed in the field of literature and art ran into the army, and literature and art entered a period of silence. This period did not last long, and then political changes caused a sharp division in literature and art. The literary debate in the spring of the seventeenth year was a concrete manifestation, and since then, the youth's view of literature and art has been distressed in theory. To this day, many young people have gone into confusion. This presents a bad symptom in national culture. In the past, young people made considerable efforts in literature and art. This is undeniable, but their mistakes are indeed numerous. First, from the perspective of literature and art itself, the general youth's demand for literature and art is aesthetic enjoyment. Therefore, the atmosphere of emotion and personality is very strong, and they forget the elements of the era and socialization. They believe that literature and art are a spark of genius, so they only grasp fragmentary impressions and seek so-called "inspiration." They are never willing to have deep cultivation. Even though the "Palace of Art" has been evacuated recently, what has been exchanged is a rigid theory of social science, which has become a passive megaphone. The erroneous views on literature and art are still the same as before. Second, from the attitude of engaging in literature and art, many young people engage in literary and artistic work, not because they have nothing to do, but because they want to spend their time or are willing to be special tools. At the same time, there are many young people who regard engaging in literature and art as a "knocking brick." When they have not found the door to enter, they work very hard in literature and art. However, once an idol is created and there is another important position, they abandon literature and art like discarded shoes or even change their minds before they become famous and abandon it to go elsewhere.

Looking Up (Photographed by Chang I An) 218

In conclusion, it is always impossible to regard literature and art as a lifelong career. These are obvious phenomena in the past, but they are bad and wrong phenomena, which are harmful to national culture.

We examine the above errors and can get a common place, that is, we have not regarded literature and art as something about national culture. Only in this way, in the first place, do we only regard literature and art as two extremes, either personal or class. Therefore, we are not willing to consciously cultivate ourselves. In the second place, we are also irrelevant and only think in a narrow place, and do not recognize it as a sacred spiritual undertaking. If these two mistakes are not corrected, it will not only be a chronic illness of the literary world, but also a crucial part of national culture. But how to correct it? This question can already be seen from the above, that is, we should first determine the central consciousness of literature and art, and this central consciousness is undoubtedly the national consciousness, in other words, taking national culture as the standpoint. We know that in the distant beginning of history, art did not originate from personal consciousness but from the consciousness of life formed from the standpoint of the nation. The important mission of literature and art is to develop the national spirit and consciousness to which it belongs. At the same time, only the development of literature and art, which is the highest expression of national culture, can make the life of the nation upward, the spirit improved, and the society progressive. The Chinese nation is now suffering from all kinds of oppression, and the domestic literary world is taking the path of that abnormal development, with crises lurking everywhere. Therefore, the establishment of national consciousness in literature and art today is absolutely necessary. Young people who love literature and art, free yourselves from the distress of your literary theories, recognize your current task. This current task is the affirmation of national consciousness to actively develop the national strength and create a new life for the nation.

What is the Purpose of Young People Studying? 219

Bringing up this question for discussion, some people may laugh at me for being bored. However, this question is closely related to the youth themselves and the future of the nation. It is more meaningful for us to discuss it than to discuss any other question.

Some people say that young people study for their own sake. Young people must have a foothold in society, find their own way out, and solve all their own problems. All of this requires studying. Therefore, friends who are doing sweet love dreams must also study to solve their love problems. Friends who are dissatisfied with the status quo must also study in order to seek their future golden age. Friends who have no status in society and rely on others' breath must also enroll in order to obtain special status and satisfy their desire for control. Needless to say, friends who are at the end of their rope must also enroll. There are many future paths to promotion and wealth. Honestly speaking, which young person's study is not for his own selfishness? However, this kind of extremely individualistic study, the result of selfishness and self-interest, is greatly detrimental to the development of the nation's future. At the same time, the young people themselves have less benefits and more losses.

Some people say that young people study for the sake of society. There are too many problems in society waiting for young people to solve. Young people study in order to use knowledge as a tool to solve social problems. Who can say that he is not? Therefore, young people who believe in socialism must enroll. They can wear suits, eat big meals, sit in automobiles, and stroll around dance halls while talking about their class struggle, go to coffee shops, open big hotels, sit under electric fans, and do proletarian literature. The result of this kind of extremely socialist study is to announce the death penalty for society and dig graves for oneself.

Finally, we should advocate that young people study for the sake of the nation. We are an oppressed nation. To obtain a free and equal position from an oppressed position, this important mission has fallen on our shoulders. We are studying in order to save the Chinese nation from danger. We are studying in order to seek the development of the Chinese nation. Young people who study natural science should strive for the development of material civilization to solve the four major problems of the nation's clothing, food, housing, and transportation. Young people who study social science should strive for practical knowledge of politics and law in order to improve the health of the nation's group organization and the improvement of common life. Young people who study literature and art should strive for the nationalistic literary movement to actively awaken national consciousness and promote national spirit. To sum up, we study neither for our own selfishness nor for a certain class in society nor for a narrow national concept. We study in order to seek the interests of the entire nation and find a way out in order to achieve the goal of freedom and equality. Dear

Page 22

Young people, cherish and work hard for the future of the nation. (Sword)

SVN in the Classroom 220

Mr. F, who teaches us history, is a graduate of a church university. He is probably forty years old. He is very short and his shoulders are a little bent. His eyes are very deep and his cheeks are suddenly sunken. This makes his body seem very thin and pitiful. He lacks the ability to intimidate students. Secondly, he mechanically reads a sentence of the original text and translates a sentence of Chinese, as if he were teaching an English textbook in junior high school, without adding any material outside the book, so he cannot arouse the interest of the students. Thirdly, history is fundamentally about settling old accounts, especially Western history is very complicated, and most students get a headache when they listen to it. So, except for a few people who are particularly interested in history, the rest of the students do not listen to the class. As soon as the bell rings for class, Mr. F immediately runs into the classroom. At this time, the classroom is so quiet that there is not even a single person. He puts the book on the desk, opens the roll book, pulls out the pen tube of the fountain pen, puts it on the roll book, and waits quietly. After two minutes, the student masters slowly come with their books.

Strangely, although there are very few people who listen to his class attentively, everyone is present when he calls the roll. Very few people are absent. This has to be thanked to a motto, "Go to class for roll call."

After the roll call, the teacher turns the book over and teaches sentence by sentence. At this time, some people are looking down intently at novels, some are flipping through newspapers at will, and some are talking in low voices. Only a few people are raising their heads and opening their mouths, listening attentively. "The price of gold is rising sharply, almost breaking through the 600 tael mark." One student, whose father is from the Gold Exchange, said to another student.

"That's right. As soon as the price of gold rises, everything becomes expensive. The books of the Commercial Press will also be sold at the real price, and we will have an extra expense in vain." Another student seems to be full of emotion.

"Excuse me, can I borrow your newspaper?"

He took the newspaper and flipped through it at will, and then looked for it in detail in the local news, saying in a surprised and distrustful tone, "Hey, there are no rape cases today."

At the same time, several other students are discussing movie stars.

"Clara Bow is really good. Her performance of innocent and lively energy is the most natural."

"What's so good about Clara Bow? I don't like her kind of frivolous energy the most. Jenny Gaynor's performance is really delicate and profound."

"I think Bibi Daniel is good."

It's really inexplicable. It has nothing to do with them, but they all like to support their favorite stars and oppose the stars that others are satisfied with. Several parties do not give in to each other, and then start a fierce debate. The voice gets louder and louder, almost forgetting that they are in the classroom.

Mr. F is a good man. As long as they talk quietly or write, he will not interfere. Now that it is too outrageous, he has to manage it, saying angrily, "If you don't want to listen, you can go out. Don't make noise in the classroom and disturb others."

In order to save Mr. F's face, everyone was silent for a while. In less than five minutes, everything was the same as before.

"Lao Wang, what are you eating?"

"Because I didn't eat, I bought a few pieces of cake."

"Give me a piece."

"Sorry, I just finished eating it."

"Don't be so stingy. It doesn't matter if you take a piece to eat."

"I really finished eating it. If you want to eat it, I will buy it for you after class."

"·············"

"·············"

Suddenly all the sounds stopped automatically. Everyone looked up at Mr. F because at this time he was reading a sentence: "Mary Stuart is a woman of remarkable beauty." Then he translated, "Mary Stuart is an unusually beautiful woman." A woman, and an unusually beautiful woman, what an attractive noun, so everyone's voices stopped.

A student who is known for being naughty stood up and said, "Mr. F, what is Mary Stuart's Faoe like?"

Mr. F is about to get angry, but he immediately feels that it is not worth it, frowning and saying, "Isn't there a picture of her here?"

This naughty student is very ignorant and still wants to ask, "Mr. F, have you seen it before?"

Mary Stuart was a woman of the sixteenth century, and Mr. F is a modern person. Never mind the difference in countries, how can anyone live so long to see a character from two centuries ago? This is obviously a thoughtless, deliberately joking, stupid question. Mr. F got angry.

"You don't ask about other important questions, but you only ask about these boring questions. Do you really have the sincerity to listen to history?"

··········

The first time the bell rang to end the class, Mr. F's words were only half said, and the students had already rushed out.

Female Poet to Enter Fudan 221

Miss Yu Xiuyun, the female poet and author of the poetry collection "Lake Breeze," has been receiving attention since we saw her name on the list of high school graduates from the Education Bureau. Because she has always been admired, we were eager to learn about her news after "Patriotism." Graduates of Liangjiang Women's Physical Education School, Zhang Huazhen and Wu Zhihong (photo by Chang Lie). The sole reason for her attention is that she is a high-achieving female poet, as well as a female athlete, possessing both poetic beauty and physical health. Recently, she created a sensation by playing a female lawyer on stage several times, inadvertently earning the informal title of "Queen," a term still carrying some feudal connotations. Given her background, pursuing higher education was never a problem. However, the question was which university she would attend. As you can see from the title, she will be entering Fudan University. Shouldn't we celebrate the arrival of another beautiful "princess" in the Eastern Palace? No, what we should celebrate is the prospect of a few short poems in publications, a healthy and unrestrained figure on the basketball court, and a moving female lead on stage. This will happen soon, as she plans to enter Fudan's summer school during the summer vacation. However, she said something along the lines of "closing the door to study and ceasing activities," which is disappointing. There may be a reason for her words. People have given her the beautiful title of "Queen," enjoying watching her and even subjecting her to some slander while wearing the crown. However, according to social psychologists, this is a normal state of society and is not surprising. Thinking about this may make one less concerned. We hope so. (Zhu Yan)

Guidelines for Youth Section Contributions 222

(1) Written submissions should be about youth issues, domestic and international school or student news, essays, school life descriptions, etc., with no restrictions on style.

(2) Illustrations should be related to youth issues.

(3) Photographs related to youth life (such as sports, travel, excursions, theatrical performances, speeches, gatherings, exhibitions, various competitions, etc.), school news, and youth movement photography are welcome, whether of individuals or groups.

(4) Do not write on both sides of the manuscript paper.

(5) The number of words per article should not exceed 2,000.

(6) Do not write horizontally or in a careless manner. Western text should be minimized; if it is necessary to quote the original, it must be attached below the translation.

(7) Do not use blue ink for illustrations, and do not use colored paper. Use white paper and black ink.

Foreign Life Amidst Rising Material Prices 223

Huo Lin Where did the six hundred taels of silver go? The price of gold is rising, the value of silver is falling, and the prices of various goods are soaring along with gold. When talking about the word "life," everyone secretly complains. Recently, a Western newspaper published an article titled "Rising Cost of Living," revealing the impact of rising prices on foreigners in Shanghai. It's easy to imagine a sense of embarrassment. It says that even if a small family of two has a monthly salary of six hundred taels of silver, their life is still difficult to maintain. Here is a detailed account of how a monthly salary of six hundred silver dollars is spent on food, clothing, and housing: The first thing is to find a place to live. A very small house or a lodge room, with no furnishings, will cost at least sixty-five or seventy-five taels in rent. Finding a place where the rent is as low as fifty taels is considered very lucky. However, how many people can find a house in the first month of the year with a rent of only forty taels of silver, including water? However, in the current situation, it is only a recollection. If we flip through the newspapers from the beginning of the year, we see a rental advertisement for a house located on Route Sayzoong, recently wallpapered, with a monthly rent of only thirty-five taels. Once you have a place to live, you need to hire servants. A cook now costs thirty to forty yuan in wages. Last year, they could be hired for twenty-five yuan. Fortunately, the price of a "boy" is as high as twenty yuan, whereas it used to be only fifteen yuan. An amah's wage must be twenty yuan. Your handkerchiefs and socks are still being pilfered, plus twenty-five yuan worth of food stolen from the kitchen. The expenses of the servants supporting their brothers, grandmothers, and friends cost eighty-five to ninety yuan. A very simple life for two people, rarely entertaining guests, still requires a monthly food bill of one hundred and twenty-five yuan. This figure does not include delicacies like olives and caviar. This figure only includes taking some vegetables and leftover roasted meat to make a mixed dish for today's lunch, and drinking a little cocktail whiskey soda and sherry, wine, and white wine when guests are present before two meals a day, then another seventy-five yuan is needed each month. It is questionable whether this amount is enough. One family of two spent seventy-two yuan last month, but they only entertained people for two meals. Electricity costs ten taels of silver per month, compared to eight taels last year. Gas is twenty-three taels, compared to fifteen taels last year. A telephone costs fifty-two taels per year, and it is said to be increasing. Tap water costs five taels of silver, with further increases expected. Using an electric refrigerator in the summer costs six hundred taels of silver. Fuel for heating in the winter costs thirty-eight yuan per month. Laundry costs twelve yuan per month for two people, compared to ten yuan in the past. Dry cleaning used to cost eight yuan, but now it costs ten yuan. If you have a car, you will need at least forty gallons of gasoline per month, which is only enough for two trips from home to the office each day, with very few pleasure drives. Six weeks ago, gasoline cost fifty-five cents per gallon, but now it costs eighty cents. Rumor has it that it will soon sell for one dollar and ten cents per gallon (currently, it has reached this amount). In this situation, it is best to leave the car in the garage and take the bus instead. Now let's talk about daily household expenses. Medicines and cosmetics, toothpaste that used to sell for seventy-five cents now cost over one yuan. Light gas for lighting used to cost one yuan per bottle a year ago, but now costs one dollar and twenty-five cents. Palm soap used to cost one dollar for five bars, but now there are only four. Aspirin costs one dollar per bottle, whereas it cost seventy-five cents six months ago. Horlick's Malted Milk costs three dollars and twenty-five cents per can, compared to two dollars and fifty cents in January. Hall's Hair Renewer costs five dollars, whereas it used to cost three dollars and fifty cents. Pond's Cold Cream costs two dollars and fifty cents per jar, compared to two dollars in the past. Hand lotion costs one dollar and seventy-five cents, which is essential in Shanghai, compared to one dollar and twenty-five cents in January. Colgate shaving soap costs one dollar per tube, compared to seventy-five cents in the past. Gillette razor blades now cost two dollars and fifty cents, compared to two dollars in the past. Listerine mouthwash has increased significantly from two dollars to two dollars and ninety cents. Face powder now costs five dollars and fifty cents per box, compared to four dollars in the past. Lipstick costs one dollar and seventy-five cents, compared to one dollar and thirty cents in the past. Rouge costs the same. In this year, using a small jar of perfume is a real luxury. Clothes are essential, although in this weather, it is best not to wear clothes. In foreign-run stores, women's shoes cost from thirty-one dollars and fifty cents to thirty-seven dollars and fifty cents. Men's boots cost from eighteen dollars and fifty cents to thirty-eight dollars and fifty cents. Footwear has increased by 25% in the past six months. Silk stockings cost seven dollars and fifty cents per pair but are not durable. More durable stockings cost five dollars and thirty cents. Ordinary stockings usually cost three dollars and fifty cents to five dollars. A stylish tie now costs eight yuan. In the past, this amount could buy three pairs of socks costing one dollar and seventy-five cents to three dollars and seventy-five cents, which is lucky, but is already a 25% increase from the past. A set of high-quality clothes made of Scottish wool costs an average of one hundred and thirty-five yuan. Last year, the same quality would have cost one hundred and ten yuan. High-quality hats cost twenty-eight dollars and fifty cents, compared to twenty-one to twenty-two yuan last year. Palm Beach suits cost forty-two yuan, compared to thirty-seven yuan in the past. White flannel costs sixty-five yuan, compared to fifty-five yuan in the past. A person should have at least six sets of clothes in the summer, and preferably twelve. Shirts have increased by two yuan since last year, and better quality shirts cost fourteen dollars and fifty cents. BVDs cost four dollars and ninety cents, compared to three dollars and fifty cents last year. The material used for a set of thin pajamas is about the same as a set of clothes, so each set costs eighteen dollars and fifty cents, compared to sixteen dollars and fifty cents last year. A person often hears that "summer dresses" are cheap. Organdy is a great material for making evening outerwear in this summer. Each yard costs two dollars and fifty cents. Of course, a person can buy six yards of it, take it to a tailor, and have them make a tight-fitting, connected skirt that looks very elegant on the body, as if waiting for her lover at the park entrance. This would cost thirty yuan. If you want something dazzling and unique, then a French-style blouse will cost eighty-five to one hundred yuan. Silk clothes cost at least one hundred yuan in high-end stores. It costs six to twelve yuan per yard. High-quality Chiva Ghee costs seven yuan and forty cents per yard. A person can make a dress with two and a half yards of material, but the style and workmanship will be lacking. If summer clothes are cheap, of course, many women will have to prepare to change clothes every three days. In this way, a person must have twelve washed long clothes, as well as clothes for banquets and dances. Hats are very expensive. Something that catches the eye always costs thirty yuan. The cheapest hat costs at least twenty yuan. A woman must have several hats in order to cope.

The Market

Business News 224

Wei Ya Restaurant, located at the intersection of North Sichuan Road and Chongming Road and No. 4 Simalu, claims that the restaurant has been open for more than ten years. Every summer, they specially hire famous vegetarian chefs to cook various special Cantonese vegetarian dishes, which have been warmly welcomed by all sectors. This year, they have further researched and refined their offerings to meet the refined tastes of their customers. They are officially launching their menu today, with a variety of dishes priced from twelve yuan to fifty yuan. Other small drinks are priced cheaply, calculated in small foreign currency, making them both affordable and delicious. Jiangsu Bank claims that the bank was founded in the first year of the Republic of China and operates all banking businesses, including savings. Its business has always been exceptionally prosperous and its reputation is well-known. In order to expand its business and provide convenience to customers, it has specially added a branch office at the east end of the Xin Zha Road and Wu Zhen Road Bridge (west of Jiangyuan Lane), with Mr. Zhu Kuiyuan as the director. Mr. Zhu is a pioneer in the financial industry, and his business is sure to develop in the future. Preparations are already underway and it will open soon. China Leather Company claims that because the company shipped too many raw materials for suitcases from the United States, it is holding a special grand sale for one month. Tomorrow is the last day for cheap prices. Please pay attention if you need high-quality and indestructible suitcases for export. Du Jinsheng Silk Weaving Factory on North Sichuan Road claims that the factory will hold a summer sale for one month starting on July 1st. All of the factory's famous products, such as silk woven scenery, colorful embroidered lapel underwear, and Western-style eyeglass frames, will be on sale. Miao Ji Department Store on North Sichuan Road claims that since its founding ten years ago, the company has always adhered to the business philosophy of honesty and trustworthiness, selling at low profits, which has been well received by society. July 1st marks the company's ninth anniversary, so a grand sale will be held for thirty-one days starting on the 1st. Exquisite gifts, including more than thirty large prizes and more than three thousand small prizes, will be presented to customers using a lottery method as a souvenir. The types of gifts and detailed rules will be published in a special supplement to the Shen Bao tomorrow to inform everyone.

Theater News 225

Xi Shen Film Company claims that its new film "Lipstick Hero" has been completely filmed and is of excellent quality. It is the company's most exciting product and the masterpiece of director Hu Zongli. Martial arts actress Wang Feijuan plays the daughter of a martial artist in the film, experiencing various difficulties and single-handedly saving her father. The plot is very tortuous. Shanghai Film Company claims that the film "Tofu Xishi," produced by the company and directed by Du Yu, starring Yin Mingzhu and Yuan Nongmei, will be released at the Central Grand Theater starting tomorrow (2nd). The plot of this film is extremely popular and the description is extremely clear. It initially depicts the vanity of a poor girl, then describes her indulging in singing and dancing and forgetting to return. Finally, it describes her regaining her original self after being subjected to various stimuli. The writing is both painful and profound, with a warning and inspiration. The Shanghai Girls' Glamorous Dance Troupe will be performing day and night, with nearly twenty actors. The play is titled "Magu Offering Longevity," an old play done in a new way, with excellent singing and dancing, as well as luxurious scenery, which is particularly outstanding.
